    $importantElem.click();
  }

     $("body").on("mousedown",  function (e){
        if ($(".tooltip-text-fake").length > 0) {
            if ($(e.target).hasClass("tooltip-icon-check-fake")) {
               var idCheckbox = $(e.target).attr("data-id-check");
               var checkBoxThis = $(e.target).parent().find("input")
               if (checkBoxThis.prop("checked")) {
                  return false;
               }
            }

            var that = $(".tooltip-text-fake");
            if (!that.is(e.target) && that.has(e.target).length === 0) {
              $(".tooltip-hidden-fake").each(function() {
                  $(this).prop('checked',false)
              })
            }
        }
    });
    $("body").on("click", ".tooltip-icon-check-fake", function(e){

          var idCheckbox = $(this).attr("data-id-check");

          var checkBoxThis = $(e.target).parent().find("input")
          if (checkBoxThis.prop("checked")) {
              checkBoxThis.prop("checked", false)
          } else {
              checkBoxThis.prop("checked", true)
          }

      })
});

PrimeFaces.widget.Password = PrimeFaces.widget.BaseWidget.extend({
    init: function(a) {
        this._super(a);
        this.cfg.showPassword = false;

        if (!this.jq.is(":disabled")) {
            if (this.cfg.feedback) {
                this.setupFeedback()
            }
            PrimeFaces.skinInput(this.jq)
        }
        if (this.jq.hasClass("ui-toggle-password")) {
            this.buildBtnToggle();
        }
    },
    buildBtnToggle: function() {

        var a = this;
        var btn = $("<div/>", {
            "class": "btn-toggle-password",
            on: {
                click: function(event) {

                    if ($(this).hasClass("btn-toggle-password-off")) {
                        $(this).parent().find(" .ui-password").attr("type", "password")
                        $(this).removeClass("btn-toggle-password-off")
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent().find(" .ui-password").attr("type", "text")
                        $(this).addClass("btn-toggle-password-off")
                    }
                }
            }
        })
        a.jq.after(btn)
    },
    setupFeedback: function() {
        var a = this;
        var d = $(this.jqId + "_panel");
        if (d.length == 1) {
            d.remove()
        }
        this.cfg.promptLabel = this.cfg.promptLabel || "Please enter a password";
        this.cfg.weakLabel = this.cfg.weakLabel || "Weak";
        this.cfg.goodLabel = this.cfg.goodLabel || "Medium";
        this.cfg.strongLabel = this.cfg.strongLabel || "Strong";
        var e = this.cfg.inline ? "ui-password-panel-inline" : "ui-password-panel-overlay";
        var c = '<div id="' + this.id + '_panel" class="ui-password-panel ui-widget ui-state-highlight ui-corner-all ui-helper-hidden ' + e + '">';
        c += '<div class="ui-password-meter" style="background-position:0pt 0pt">&nbsp;</div>';
        c += '<div class="ui-password-info">' + this.cfg.promptLabel + "</div>";
        c += "</div>";
        this.panel = $(c).insertAfter(this.jq);
        this.meter = this.panel.children("div.ui-password-meter");
        this.infoText = this.panel.children("div.ui-password-info");
        if (!this.cfg.inline) {
            this.panel.addClass("ui-shadow")
        }
        this.jq.focus(function() {
            a.show()
        }).blur(function() {
            a.hide()
        }).keyup(function() {
            var h = a.jq.val()
              , f = null
              , g = null;
            if (h.length == 0) {
                f = a.cfg.promptLabel;
                g = "0px 0px"
            } else {
                var i = a.testStrength(a.jq.val());
                if (i < 30) {
                    f = a.cfg.weakLabel;
                    g = "0px -10px"
                } else {
                    if (i >= 30 && i < 80) {
                        f = a.cfg.goodLabel;
                        g = "0px -20px"
                    } else {
                        if (i >= 80) {
                            f = a.cfg.strongLabel;
                            g = "0px -30px"
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            a.meter.css("background-position", g);
            a.infoText.text(f)
        });
        if (!this.cfg.inline) {
            this.panel.appendTo("body");
            var b = "resize." + this.id;
            $(window).unbind(b).bind(b, function() {
                if (a.panel.is(":visible")) {
                    a.align()
                }
            })
        }
    },
    testStrength: function(d) {
        var b = 0
          , c = 0
          , a = this;
        c = d.match("[0-9]");
        b += a.normalize(c ? c.length : 1 / 4, 1) * 25;
        c = d.match("[a-zA-Z]");
        b += a.normalize(c ? c.length : 1 / 2, 3) * 10;
        c = d.match("[!@#$%^&*?_~.,;=]");
        b += a.normalize(c ? c.length : 1 / 6, 1) * 35;
        c = d.match("[A-Z]");
        b += a.normalize(c ? c.length : 1 / 6, 1) * 30;
        b *= d.length / 8;
        return b > 100 ? 100 : b
    },
    normalize: function(a, c) {
        var b = a - c;
        if (b <= 0) {
            return a / c
        } else {
            return 1 + 0.5 * (a / (a + c / 4))
        }
    },
    align: function() {
        this.panel.css({
            left: "",
            top: "",
            "z-index": ++PrimeFaces.zindex
        }).position({
            my: "left top",
            at: "right top",
            of: this.jq
        })
    },
    show: function() {
        if (!this.cfg.inline) {
            this.align();
            this.panel.fadeIn()
        } else {
            this.panel.slideDown()
        }
    },
    hide: function() {
        if (this.cfg.inline) {
            this.panel.slideUp()
        } else {
            this.panel.fadeOut()
        }
    }
});
PrimeFaces.dialog.DialogHandler.openDialog = function (cfg) {

    var rootWindow = PrimeFaces.dialog.DialogHandler.findRootWindow();
    dialogId = cfg.sourceComponentId + '_dlg';

    var dragWindow = false

    if ($("[id='" + cfg.sourceComponentId + "']").closest("[id$='workplaceForm:dataObjectSectionsContainer:dataObjectControllerInstanceFields__indInteg__Value']").length > 0) {
        dragWindow = true
    }


    if (rootWindow.document.getElementById(dialogId)) {
        return;
    }

    var dialogWidgetVar = cfg.sourceComponentId.replace(/:/g, '_') + '_dlgwidget',
        styleClass = cfg.options.styleClass || '',
        dialogDOM = $('<div id="' + dialogId + '" class="ui-dialog ui-widget ui-widget-content ui-corner-all ui-shadow ui-hidden-container custom-dialog ui-overlay-hidden ' + styleClass + '"' +
            ' data-pfdlgcid="' + cfg.pfdlgcid + '" data-widgetvar="' + dialogWidgetVar + '"></div>')
            .append('<div class="ui-dialog-titlebar ui-widget-header ui-helper-clearfix ui-corner-top"><span class="ui-dialog-title"></span></div>');

    var titlebar = dialogDOM.children('.ui-dialog-titlebar');
    if (cfg.options.closable !== false) {
        titlebar.append('<a class="ui-dialog-titlebar-icon ui-dialog-titlebar-close ui-corner-all" href="#" role="button"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-closethick"></span></a>');
    }

    if (cfg.options.minimizable) {
        titlebar.append('<a class="ui-dialog-titlebar-icon ui-dialog-titlebar-minimize ui-corner-all" href="#" role="button"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-minus"></span></a>');
    }

    if (cfg.options.maximizable) {
        titlebar.append('<a class="ui-dialog-titlebar-icon ui-dialog-titlebar-maximize ui-corner-all" href="#" role="button"><span class="ui-icon ui-icon-extlink"></span></a>');
    }

    dialogDOM.append('<div class="ui-dialog-content ui-widget-content ui-df-content" style="height: auto;">' +
        '<iframe style="border:0 none" frameborder="0"/>' +
        '</div>');

    dialogDOM.appendTo(rootWindow.document.body);

    var dialogFrame = dialogDOM.find('iframe'),
        symbol = cfg.url.indexOf('?') === -1 ? '?' : '&',
        frameURL = cfg.url.indexOf('pfdlgcid') === -1 ? cfg.url + symbol + 'pfdlgcid=' + cfg.pfdlgcid : cfg.url,
        frameWidth = cfg.options.contentWidth || 640;



    dialogFrame.width(frameWidth);

    if (cfg.options.iframeTitle) {
        dialogFrame.attr('title', cfg.options.iframeTitle);
    }

    dialogFrame.on('load', function () {
        var $frame = $(this),
            headerElement = $frame.contents().find('title'),
            isCustomHeader = false;
			$($frame.contents().find("body")).addClass("frame-window");

        var style = $("[attrmaincss='true']").clone();
        	$frame.contents().find("head").append(style);

        var jsTag = $("[attrmainjs='true']").clone();
      		$frame.contents().find("head").append(jsTag);
			$frame.contents().find("head link[href*='theme.css']").remove();
            $frame.contents().find("head link[href*='add.less']").remove();
            $frame.contents().find("head link[href*='mini-screen.less']").remove();
            $frame.contents().find("head link[href*='layout.less']").remove();
            $frame.contents().find("head link[href*='screen.css']").remove();
       		$($frame.contents()).ready(function(){

				$($frame.contents()).on("auxclick contextmenu ", "a", function(e) {
                  e.preventDefault();
                  return false;
                })
                $($frame.contents()).on("click", "a", function(e) {
                  if (e.ctrlKey || e.shiftKey) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    return false;
                  }
                })

			})

      	$frame.contents().find("head").append("<div class='hidden-bodyModel'><style>body  {visibility: hidden; opacity: 0;}</style></div>");


        if (cfg.options.headerElement) {
            var customHeaderId = PrimeFaces.escapeClientId(cfg.options.headerElement),
                customHeaderElement = dialogFrame.contents().find(customHeaderId);

            if (customHeaderElement.length) {
                headerElement = customHeaderElement;
                isCustomHeader = true;
            }
        }

        if (!$frame.data('initialized')) {

            if (dragWindow) {
                PrimeFaces.cw.call(rootWindow.PrimeFaces, 'DynamicDialog', dialogWidgetVar, {
                    id: dialogId,
                    position: '200, 100',
                    sourceComponentId: cfg.sourceComponentId,
                    sourceWidgetVar: cfg.sourceWidgetVar,
                    onHide: function () {
                        var $dialogWidget = this,
                            dialogFrame = this.content.children('iframe');

                        if (dialogFrame.get(0).contentWindow.PrimeFaces) {
                            this.destroyIntervalId = setInterval(function () {
                                if (dialogFrame.get(0).contentWindow.PrimeFaces.ajax.Queue.isEmpty()) {
                                    clearInterval($dialogWidget.destroyIntervalId);
                                    dialogFrame.attr('src', 'about:blank');
                                    $dialogWidget.jq.remove();
                                }
                            }, 10);
                        }
                        else {
                            dialogFrame.attr('src', 'about:blank');
                            $dialogWidget.jq.remove();
                        }

                        rootWindow.PF[dialogWidgetVar] = undefined;
                    },
                    modal: cfg.options.modal,
                    resizable: cfg.options.resizable,
                    hasIframe: true,
                    draggable: true,

                    width: '600',
                    height: '500',
                    minimizable: cfg.options.minimizable,
                    maximizable: cfg.options.maximizable,
                    headerElement: cfg.options.headerElement,
                    responsive: cfg.options.responsive,
                    closeOnEscape: cfg.options.closeOnEscape
                });

            } else {
                PrimeFaces.cw.call(rootWindow.PrimeFaces, 'DynamicDialog', dialogWidgetVar, {
                    id: dialogId,
                    position: cfg.options.position || 'center',
                    sourceComponentId: cfg.sourceComponentId,
                    sourceWidgetVar: cfg.sourceWidgetVar,
                    onHide: function () {
                        var $dialogWidget = this,
                            dialogFrame = this.content.children('iframe');

                        if (dialogFrame.get(0).contentWindow.PrimeFaces) {
                            this.destroyIntervalId = setInterval(function () {
                                if (dialogFrame.get(0).contentWindow.PrimeFaces.ajax.Queue.isEmpty()) {
                                    clearInterval($dialogWidget.destroyIntervalId);
                                    dialogFrame.attr('src', 'about:blank');
                                    $dialogWidget.jq.remove();
                                }
                            }, 10);
                        }
                        else {
                            dialogFrame.attr('src', 'about:blank');
                            $dialogWidget.jq.remove();
                        }

                        rootWindow.PF[dialogWidgetVar] = undefined;
                    },
                    modal: cfg.options.modal,
                    resizable: cfg.options.resizable,
                    hasIframe: true,
                  	styleClass: "wwwww" ,
                    draggable: cfg.options.draggable,
                    width: cfg.options.width,
                    height: cfg.options.height,
                    minimizable: cfg.options.minimizable,
                    maximizable: cfg.options.maximizable,
                    headerElement: cfg.options.headerElement,
                    responsive: cfg.options.responsive,
                    closeOnEscape: cfg.options.closeOnEscape
                });
            }
        }



        var title = rootWindow.PF(dialogWidgetVar).titlebar.children('span.ui-dialog-title');
        if (headerElement.length > 0) {
            if (isCustomHeader) {
                title.append(headerElement);
                headerElement.show();
            }
            else {
                title.text(headerElement.text());
            }

            dialogFrame.attr('title', title.text());
        }

        //adjust height
        var frameHeight = null;
        if (cfg.options.contentHeight)
            frameHeight = cfg.options.contentHeight;
        else
            frameHeight = $frame.get(0).contentWindow.document.body.scrollHeight + (PrimeFaces.env.browser.webkit ? 5 : 25);

        $frame.css('height', frameHeight);

        // fix #1290 - dialogs are not centered vertically
        dialogFrame.data('initialized', true);
        rootWindow.PF(dialogWidgetVar).show();

        //only for these 2 rows
        if (cfg.options.maximized)
            rootWindow.PF(dialogWidgetVar).toggleMaximize();

		if (dragWindow) {
          	$("[id$='" + dialogId + "']").addClass("centerAndGradCustom");
		    $(".centerAndGradCustom").css({
				'left': Math.floor(window.outerWidth * 0.1) + "px",
				'top': Math.floor(window.outerHeight * 0.22) + "px"})
		}
        window.setTimeout(function(){
        	$frame.contents().find(".hidden-bodyModel").remove();
            if ($frame[0].contentWindow["autoFocusInputIFrame"]) {
                $frame[0].contentWindow.autoFocusInputIFrame();
            }
            if ($frame.contents().find(".modelPage .ui-datatable-footer.ui-widget-header").length > 0) {
                $frame.contents().find(".modelPage .ui-datatable-footer.ui-widget-header").removeAttr("style");
            }

        }, 1000);


    })
        .attr('src', frameURL);


console.log("Open dialog window within iframe");


};

PrimeFaces.widget.Slider = PrimeFaces.widget.BaseWidget.extend({
    init: function(b) {
        this._super(b);
        if (this.jq.attr("listvalues")) {

            if (this.cfg.value % 1 == 0) {
                this.cfg.value = parseInt(this.cfg.value, 10)+"";
            }
            this.cfg.value = this.jq.attr("listvalues").split(":").indexOf(this.cfg.value);
        }
        this.cfg.displayTemplate = this.cfg.displayTemplate || (this.cfg.range ? "{min} - {max}" : "{value}");
        if (this.cfg.range) {
            var a = this.cfg.input.split(",");
            this.input = $(PrimeFaces.escapeClientId(a[0]) + "," + PrimeFaces.escapeClientId(a[1]))
        } else {
            this.input = $(PrimeFaces.escapeClientId(this.cfg.input))
        }
        if (this.cfg.display) {
            this.output = $(PrimeFaces.escapeClientId(this.cfg.display))
        }
        this.jq.slider(this.cfg);
        this.bindEvents();
        if (PrimeFaces.env.touch) {
            this.bindTouchEvents()
        }

      	this.jq.append("<span class='blue-line-slider'></span>");
        $(this.jq.find(".blue-line-slider")).css("width", $(this.jq.find(".ui-slider-handle")).position().left + "px");
      	if (this.jq.width() == 0) {
        	$(this.jq.find(".blue-line-slider")).css("width", "0px");
        }
        this.setColourPoints();
    },
    bindEvents: function() {
        var a = this;

          if (this.jq.attr("listvalues")) {

            a.buildPoint();
          }

          this.jq.bind("slide", function(b, c) {
            a.onSlide(b, c)
          });
          if (this.cfg.onSlideStart) {
            this.jq.bind("slidestart", function(b, c) {
              a.cfg.onSlideStart.call(this, b, c)
            })
          }
          this.jq.bind("slidestop", function(b, c) {
            a.onSlideEnd(b, c)
          });
          if (this.input.parent().hasClass("ui-inputnumber")) {
            this.input.parent().find("input:hidden").on("change", function() {
              a.setValue($(this).val())
            })
          } else {
            this.input.on("keydown.slider", function(f) {
              var d = $.ui.keyCode
              , c = f.which;
              switch (c) {
                case d.UP:
                case d.DOWN:
                case d.LEFT:
                case d.RIGHT:
                case d.BACKSPACE:
                case d.DELETE:
                case d.END:
                case d.HOME:
                case d.TAB:
                  break;
                default:
                  var g = f.metaKey || f.ctrlKey
                  , b = (c >= 48 && c <= 57) || (c >= 96 && c <= 105);
                  if (f.altKey || (f.shiftKey && !(c === d.UP || c === d.DOWN || c === d.LEFT || c === d.RIGHT))) {
                    f.preventDefault()
                  }
                  if (!b && !g) {
                    f.preventDefault()
                  }
                  break
                       }
            }).on("keyup.slider", function(b) {
              a.setValue(a.input.val())
            })
          }
    },
    bindTouchEvents: function() {
        var a = {
            touchstart: "mousedown",
            touchmove: "mousemove",
            touchend: "mouseup"
        };
        this.jq.children(".ui-slider-handle").on("touchstart touchmove touchend", function(c) {
            var d = c.originalEvent.changedTouches[0];
            var b = document.createEvent("MouseEvent");
            b.initMouseEvent(a[c.originalEvent.type], true, true, window, 1, d.screenX, d.screenY, d.clientX, d.clientY, false, false, false, false, 0, null);
            d.target.dispatchEvent(b);
            c.preventDefault()
        })
    },
    onSlide: function(a, b) {
        if (this.cfg.onSlide) {
            this.cfg.onSlide.call(this, a, b)
        }
        if (this.cfg.range) {
            this.setInputValue(this.input.eq(0), b.values[0]);
            this.setInputValue(this.input.eq(1), b.values[1]);
            if (this.output) {
                this.output.html(this.cfg.displayTemplate.replace("{min}", b.values[0]).replace("{max}", b.values[1]))
            }
        } else {
            this.setInputValue(this.input, b.value);
            if (this.output) {
                this.output.html(this.cfg.displayTemplate.replace("{value}", b.value))
            }
        }

		// -------
		$(this.jq.find(".blue-line-slider")).css("width", $(this.jq.find(".ui-slider-handle")).position().left + "px");
    this.setColourPoints();
    },
    buildPoint: function () {

      var $this = this.jq;
      var points = $this.attr("listvalues").split(":");
      this.cfg.points = points;
      var parent = $this;
      var piecePath = 100 / (points.length - 1);
      var progress = 0;

      for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {
        var elem = $('<span/>', {
            class: 'slider-point',
    		    css: {
              left: progress + "%",
              position: "absolute",
            },
            append: $('<span>', {
              text: points[i]
            })
    	  })
        elem.attr("data-progress", progress);
      	$this.append(elem);
        progress += piecePath;
      }

    },
    setColourPoints: function() {

      if (this.jq.attr("listvalues")) {
        var $this = this;
        var points = $this.cfg.points;
        var listPoint = $this.jq.find(".slider-point");
        var wBlueLine = $this.jq.find(".blue-line-slider").width();
        var wSlider = $this.jq.width();
        var currentPercent =  wBlueLine / (wSlider / 100);
		if ($this.jq.width() > 0) {
          listPoint.each(function(index) {
            $(this).removeClass("bluePoint");
          })

          for (var i = 0; i < points.length; i++) {
            if($(listPoint[i]).attr("data-progress") <= currentPercent) {
              $(listPoint[i]).addClass("bluePoint");
            }
          }
        }
      }
    },
    setInputValue: function(b, a) {
        if (this.jq.attr("listvalues")) {
            if (b.parent().hasClass("ui-inputnumber")) {
              b.autoNumeric("set", this.cfg.points[a])
            } else {
              b.val(this.cfg.points[a])
            }
          } else {
            if (b.parent().hasClass("ui-inputnumber")) {
              b.autoNumeric("set", a)
            } else {
              b.val(a)
            }
          }
		// -------
		  $(this.jq.find(".blue-line-slider")).css("width", $(this.jq.find(".ui-slider-handle")).position().left + "px");
      this.setColourPoints();
    },
    triggerOnchange: function(a) {
        if (a.parent().hasClass("ui-inputnumber")) {
            a.change()
        }
    },
    onSlideEnd: function(c, d) {
        if (this.cfg.onSlideEnd) {
            this.cfg.onSlideEnd.call(this, c, d)
        }
        if (this.cfg.range) {
            this.triggerOnchange(this.input.eq(0));
            this.triggerOnchange(this.input.eq(1))
        } else {
            this.triggerOnchange(this.input)
        }
        if (this.cfg.behaviors) {
            var a = this.cfg.behaviors.slideEnd;
            if (a) {
                var b = {
                    params: [{
                        name: this.id + "_slideValue",
                        value: d.value
                    }]
                };
                a.call(this, b)
            }
        }
		// -------
		$(this.jq.find(".blue-line-slider")).css("width", $(this.jq.find(".ui-slider-handle")).position().left + "px");
    this.setColourPoints();
    },
    getValue: function() {
        return this.jq.slider("value")
    },
    setValue: function(a) {
        this.jq.slider("value", parseFloat(a))
		// -------
		$(this.jq.find(".blue-line-slider")).css("width", $(this.jq.find(".ui-slider-handle")).position().left + "px");
    this.setColourPoints();
    },
    getValues: function() {
        return this.jq.slider("values")
    },
    setValues: function(a) {
        this.jq.slider("values", parseFloat(a))
    },
    enable: function() {
        this.jq.slider("enable")
    },
    disable: function() {
        this.jq.slider("disable")
    }
});

PrimeFaces.widget.SelectOneRadio = PrimeFaces.widget.BaseWidget.extend({

    init: function(cfg) {
        this._super(cfg);

        //custom layout
        if(this.cfg.custom) {
            this.originalInputs = this.jq.find(':radio');
            this.inputs = $('input:radio[name="' + this.id + '"].ui-radio-clone');
            this.outputs = this.inputs.parent().next('.ui-radiobutton-box');
            this.labels = $();

            //labels
            for(var i=0; i < this.outputs.length; i++) {
                this.labels = this.labels.add('label[for="' + this.outputs.eq(i).parent().attr('id') + '"]');
            }

            //update radio state
            for(var i = 0; i < this.inputs.length; i++) {
                var input = this.inputs.eq(i),
                itemindex = input.data('itemindex'),
                original = this.originalInputs.eq(itemindex);

                input.val(original.val());

                if(original.is(':checked')) {
                    input.prop('checked', true).parent().next().addClass('ui-state-active').children('.ui-radiobutton-icon')
                            .addClass('ui-icon-bullet').removeClass('ui-icon-blank');
                    input.prop('checked', true).parent().parent().addClass('ui-radio-active');
                }
            }
        }
        //regular layout
        else {
            this.outputs = this.jq.find('.ui-radiobutton-box');
            this.inputs = this.jq.find(':radio');
            this.labels = this.jq.find('label');
        }

        this.enabledInputs = this.inputs.filter(':not(:disabled)');
        this.checkedRadio = this.outputs.filter('.ui-state-active');

        this.bindEvents();

        //pfs metadata
        this.inputs.data(PrimeFaces.CLIENT_ID_DATA, this.id);



        this.inputs.each(function(index, item){
        	if ($(item).attr("checked") == "checked") {
                $(item).parent().parent().addClass("ui-radio-active");
            }
        })
    },

    bindEvents: function() {
        var $this = this;

        this.outputs.filter(':not(.ui-state-disabled)').on('mouseover.selectOneRadio', function() {
            $(this).addClass('ui-state-hover');
        })
        .on('mouseout.selectOneRadio', function() {
            $(this).removeClass('ui-state-hover');
        })
        .on('click.selectOneRadio', function() {
            var radio = $(this),
            input = radio.prev().children(':radio');

            if(!radio.hasClass('ui-state-active')) {
                $this.unselect($this.checkedRadio);
                $this.select(radio);
                input.trigger('click');
                input.trigger('change');
            }
            else {
                input.trigger('click');
            }
        });

        this.labels.filter(':not(.ui-state-disabled)').on('click.selectOneRadio', function(e) {
            var target = $(PrimeFaces.escapeClientId($(this).attr('for'))),
            radio = null;

            //checks if target is input or not(custom labels)
            if(target.is(':input'))
                radio = target.parent().next();
            else
                radio = target.children('.ui-radiobutton-box'); //custom layout

            radio.trigger('click.selectOneRadio');

            e.preventDefault();
        });

        this.enabledInputs.on('focus.selectOneRadio', function() {
            var input = $(this),
            radio = input.parent().next();

            if(input.prop('checked')) {
                radio.parent().removeClass('ui-radio-active');
                radio.removeClass('ui-state-active');
            }

            radio.addClass('ui-state-focus');
        })
        .on('blur.selectOneRadio', function() {
            var input = $(this),
            radio = input.parent().next();

            if(input.prop('checked')) {
                radio.parent().addClass('ui-radio-active');
                radio.addClass('ui-state-active');
            }

            radio.removeClass('ui-state-focus');
        })
        .on('keydown.selectOneRadio', function(e) {
            var input = $(this),
            currentRadio = input.parent().next(),
            index = $this.enabledInputs.index(input),
            size = $this.enabledInputs.length,
            keyCode = $.ui.keyCode,
            key = e.which;

            switch(key) {
                case keyCode.UP:
                case keyCode.LEFT:
                	index = index - 1;
                    var fakeSize = size - 1;
                    var prevRadioInput = (index === 0) ? $this.enabledInputs.eq(fakeSize) : $this.enabledInputs.eq(index);
                    var prevRadio = prevRadioInput.parent().next();

                    input.blur();
                    $this.unselect(currentRadio);
                    $this.select(prevRadio);
                    prevRadioInput.trigger('focus').trigger('change');
                    e.preventDefault();
                break;

                case keyCode.DOWN:
                case keyCode.RIGHT:
                	index = index + 1;
                    var fakeSize = size - 1;
                    var nextRadioInput = (index === fakeSize) ? $this.enabledInputs.eq(0) : $this.enabledInputs.eq(index),
                    nextRadio = nextRadioInput.parent().next();

                    input.blur();
                    $this.unselect(currentRadio);
                    $this.select(nextRadio);
                    nextRadioInput.trigger('focus').trigger('change');
                    e.preventDefault();
                break;

                case keyCode.SPACE:
                    if(!input.prop('checked')) {
                        $this.select(currentRadio);
                        input.trigger('focus').trigger('change');
                    }

                    e.preventDefault();
                break;
            }
        });
    },

    unselect: function(radio) {
        radio.prev().children(':radio').prop('checked', false);
        radio.parent().removeClass('ui-radio-active');
        radio.removeClass('ui-state-active').children('.ui-radiobutton-icon').removeClass('ui-icon-bullet').addClass('ui-icon-blank');
    },

    select: function(radio) {
        this.checkedRadio = radio;
        radio.parent().addClass('ui-radio-active');
        radio.addClass('ui-state-active').children('.ui-radiobutton-icon').addClass('ui-icon-bullet').removeClass('ui-icon-blank');
        radio.prev().children(':radio').prop('checked', true);
    },

    unbindEvents: function(input) {
        if(input) {
            input.off();
            input.parent().nextAll('.ui-radiobutton-box').off();
            this.labels.filter("label[for='" + input.attr('id') + "']").off();
        }
        else {
            this.inputs.off();
            this.labels.off();
            this.outputs.off();
        }
    },

    disable: function(index) {
        if(index == null) {
            this.inputs.attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            this.labels.addClass('ui-state-disabled');
            this.outputs.addClass('ui-state-disabled');
            this.unbindEvents();
        }
        else {
            var input = this.inputs.eq(index),
                label = this.labels.filter("label[for='" + input.attr('id') + "']");
            input.attr('disabled', 'disabled').parent().nextAll('.ui-radiobutton-box').addClass('ui-state-disabled');
            label.addClass('ui-state-disabled');
            this.unbindEvents(input);
        }

    },

    enable: function(index) {
        if(index == null) {
            this.inputs.removeAttr('disabled');
            this.labels.removeClass('ui-state-disabled');
            this.outputs.removeClass('ui-state-disabled');
        }
        else {
            var input = this.inputs.eq(index),
                label = this.labels.filter("label[for='" + input.attr('id') + "']");
            input.removeAttr('disabled').parent().nextAll('.ui-radiobutton-box').removeClass('ui-state-disabled');
            label.removeClass('ui-state-disabled');
        }
        this.bindEvents();
    }

});

function validationPasswordUser(id, flag) {
  	if ($(".regisForm [id$='passwordPanel'] .ui-message-error.fake-error-message").length > 0 && flag) {
      $(".regisForm [id$='passwordPanel'] .ui-message-error.fake-error-message").remove();
    }
    if (!$("[data-target$='"+id+"'].ui-message-error").length > 0) {
        return;
    }

    var text = $("[id$='"+id+"']").val();

    var validationText = "<div style='color: #1C1D1F; margin-bottom: 2px;'>Пароль не соответствует требованиям безопасности. Он должен содержать:</div>";

  	if (text.length >= 8 && /(?=.*[A-Z])/.test(text) && /(?=.*[a-z])/.test(text) && /(?=.*\d)/.test(text) && /(?=.*[-.?!,:;()"\'\\/])/.test(text)) {
    	validationText = "<div style='color: #1C1D1F; margin-bottom: 2px;'>Пароль соответствует требованиям безопасности:</div>";
    }

    if (text.length < 8) {
        validationText += "<div><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: red;'></i>8 и более символов;</div>";
    } else {
        validationText += "<div style='color: #1C1D1F;'><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: #26e426;'></i>8 и более символов;</div>";
    }

    if (!/(?=.*[A-Z])/.test(text)) {
        validationText += "<div><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: red;'></i>прописные латинские буквы;</div>";
    } else {
        validationText += "<div style='color: #1C1D1F;'><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: #26e426;'></i>прописные латинские буквы;</div>";
    }

    if (!/(?=.*[a-z])/.test(text)) {
        validationText += "<div><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: red;'></i>строчные латинские буквы;</div>";
    } else {
        validationText += "<div style='color: #1C1D1F;'><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: #26e426;'></i>строчные латинские буквы;</div>";
    }

    if (!/(?=.*\d)/.test(text)) {
        validationText += "<div><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: red;'></i>цифры;</div>";
    } else {
        validationText += "<div style='color: #1C1D1F;'><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: #26e426;'></i>цифры;</div>";
    }

    if (!/(?=.*[-.?!,:;()"\'\\/])/.test(text)) {
        validationText += "<div><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: red;'></i>знаки пунктуации (-.?!,:;()\'\"/).</div>";
    } else {
        validationText += "<div style='color: #1C1D1F;'><i class='fa fa-circle' aria-hidden='true' style='color: #26e426;'></i>знаки пунктуации (-.?!,:;()\'\"/).</div>";
    }

	var flagUncurrentSymbol = false;
    for (var i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {
        if (!/[\w,:;()"'\\/!?\.-]/.test(text[i])) {
            flagUncurrentSymbol = true;
        }
    }
    if (flagUncurrentSymbol) {
        validationText = "<div style='margin-bottom: 2px;'>Введен недопустимый символ.</div><div style='color: #1C1D1F;'>Допустимые символы .?!,:;-\"()\'/.</div>";
    }

    if ($("[data-target$='"+id+"'].ui-message-error").length > 0) {
        $("[data-target$='"+id+"'].ui-message-error").css("whiteSpace" , "pre-wrap");
        $("[data-target$='"+id+"'].ui-message-error .ui-message-error-detail").html(validationText);
    }
}
function changeRowsPerPage(tablewidget, menuwidget) {
  var countRows = PF(menuwidget).jq.find(".ui-state-active input").val();
  PF(tablewidget).paginator.setRowsPerPage(countRows);
}

function replaceYearAndDay (date) {
  var newDate = date.split(".");
  return newDate[2] + "-" + newDate[1] + "-" + newDate[0];
}
function compareDateFilter(oneDate, twoDate) {
  return new Date(replaceYearAndDay(oneDate)) <= new Date(replaceYearAndDay(twoDate));
}

                    messagingSenderId: "632237793864"
                };

                firebase.initializeApp(config);

                if (!('PushManager' in window)) {
                    console.warn('Push messaging isn\'t supported.');
                    return;
                }


                messaging = firebase.messaging();
                if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
                    var wsPath = "/platform/javax.faces.resource/js/firebase-messaging-sw.js.xhtml" + "?messagingSenderId=" + config.messagingSenderId;
                    var promise = navigator.serviceWorker.register(wsPath).then(function (r) {
                        messaging.useServiceWorker(r);
                        if (pushEnabled) {
                            subscribePush();
                        }
                    }).catch(function (error) {
                        console.log('Ошибка при регистрации service worker-а:', error);
                    });

                }

                //if window active
                messaging.onMessage(function (payload) {
                    //console.log("Message received. ", payload);
                    PF('growl').renderMessage({
                        "summary": payload.notification.title,
                        "detail": payload.notification.body,
                        "severity": "info"
                    })
                });

                messaging.onTokenRefresh(function () {
                    messaging.getToken().then(function (refreshedToken) {
                        console.log('Token refreshed.');
                        sendTokenToServerAndSave(refreshedToken);
                    }).catch(function (err) {
                        console.log('Unable to retrieve refreshed token ', err);
                    });
                });

            }

            initPush();

            function subscribePush() {
                // запрашиваем разрешение на получение уведомлений
                messaging.requestPermission()
                    .then(function () {
                        // получаем ID устройства
                        messaging.getToken()
                            .then(function (currentToken) {
                                if (currentToken) {
                                    console.log(currentToken);
                                    if (!pushTokens.includes(currentToken))
                                        sendTokenToServerAndSave(currentToken);
                                } else {
                                    console.warn('Не удалось получить токен.');
                                }
                            })
                            .catch(function (err) {
                                console.warn('При получении токена произошла ошибка.', err);
                            });
                    })
                    .catch(function (err) {
                        console.warn('Не удалось получить разрешение на показ уведомлений.', err);
                    });
            }

            function unSubscribePush() {
                messaging.getToken()
                    .then(function (currentToken) {
                        messaging.deleteToken(currentToken)
                            .then(function () {
                                console.log('Token deleted');
                                removeTokenFromServer(false);
                                // Once token is deleted update UI.
                                //resetUI();
                            })
                            .catch(function (error) {
                                console.warn('Unable to delete token', error);
                            });
                    })
                    .catch(function (error) {
                        console.warn('Error retrieving Instance ID token', error);
                    });
            }

            function sendTokenToServer(currentToken) {
                addFirebaseToken([{name: 'pushToken', value: currentToken}]);
                tokens.push(currentToken);
            }

            function removeTokenFromServer(currentToken) {
                removeFirebaseToken([{name: 'pushToken', value: currentToken}]);
            }

            function sendTokenToServerAndSave(currentToken) {
                addFirebaseTokenAndSave([{name: 'pushToken', value: currentToken}]);
                console.log('new token sent to server')
            }

        </script><script id="messagesform:j_idt40" type="text/javascript">addFirebaseToken = function() {PrimeFaces.ab({s:"messagesform:j_idt40",f:"messagesform",p:"messagesform:j_idt40",g:false,pa:arguments[0]});}</script><script id="messagesform:j_idt41" type="text/javascript">addFirebaseTokenAndSave = function() {PrimeFaces.ab({s:"messagesform:j_idt41",f:"messagesform",p:"messagesform:j_idt41",g:false,pa:arguments[0]});}</script><script id="messagesform:j_idt42" type="text/javascript">removeFirebaseToken = function() {PrimeFaces.ab({s:"messagesform:j_idt42",f:"messagesform",p:"messagesform:j_idt42",g:false,pa:arguments[0]});}</script><input type="hidden" name="javax.faces.ViewState" id="j_id1:javax.faces.ViewState:0" value="-4305038174416822892:-8518443115127762521" autocomplete="off" /><input type="hidden" name="javax.faces.ClientWindow" id="j_id1:javax.faces.ClientWindow:0" value="1LTCHOPrpW-t0mY1991W0Gj00yb4D908N8Dj-XUD:0" autocomplete="off" />

    <script>
        //<![CDATA[
        function _tick(e, val, idx) {
            // console.log('val:' + val);
            // console.log('idx:' + idx);
            if ([37, 38, 39, 40].indexOf(e.keyCode) > -1) {
                if (e.keyCode == '38') {
                    // up arrow
                    if (idx > 0)
                        $('.digit' + (idx - 1)).focus();
                    else
                        $('.digit3').focus();
                } else if (e.keyCode == '40') {
                    // down arrow
                    if (idx < 3)
                        $('.digit' + (idx + 1)).focus();
                    else
                        $('.digit0').focus();
                } else if (e.keyCode == '37') {
                    // left arrow
                    if (idx > 0)
                        $('.digit' + (idx - 1)).focus();
                    else
                        $('.digit3').focus();
                } else if (e.keyCode == '39') {
                    // right arrow
                    if (idx < 3)
                        $('.digit' + (idx + 1)).focus();
                    else
                        $('.digit0').focus();
                }
                return;
            }

            if (e.key >= '0' && e.key <= '9') {
                var digits = $('.digits');
                if (idx != 3) {
                    if (val.length == 1) {
                        idx = idx + 1;
                        $('.digit' + idx).focus();
                    }
                }
                var ok = true;
                digits.each(function () {
                    if ($(this).val() === '') {
                        ok = false;
                        return ok;
                    }
                });
                if (ok) {
                    checkDigits();
                }
            }
        }

        function _isDigit(key) {
            return key >= '0' && key <= '9' || key == 'Backspace' || key == 'Delete';
        }

        var countdownTimer;

        function startTimer() {
            var timeLeft = 300;
            document.getElementById("countdown").innerHTML = timeLeft + " секунд осталось"
            countdownTimer = setInterval(function () {
                timeLeft -= 1;
                document.getElementById("countdown").innerHTML = timeLeft + " секунд осталось";
                if (timeLeft <= 0) {
                    PF('fourDigitsDialog').hide();
                }
            }, 1000);
        }

        //]]>
    </script>

                    function fixMarginRightDataTable () {

                      if (hR > 550) {
                        $("[id$='ReliabilityIndexReestrWrap'] .ui-datatable-scrollable-header-box").css("marginRight", "15px")
                      } else {
                        $("[id$='ReliabilityIndexReestrWrap'] .ui-datatable-scrollable-header-box").css("marginRight", "0")
                      }
                    }

        if (!String.prototype.padStart) {
            String.prototype.padStart = function padStart(targetLength,padString) {
                targetLength = targetLength>>0; //truncate if number or convert non-number to 0;
                padString = String((typeof padString !== 'undefined' ? padString : ' '));
                if (this.length > targetLength) {
                    return String(this);
                }
                else {
                    targetLength = targetLength-this.length;
                    if (targetLength > padString.length) {
                        padString += padString.repeat(targetLength/padString.length); //append to original to ensure we are longer than needed
                    }
                    return padString.slice(0,targetLength) + String(this);
                }
            };
        }

    <script type="application/javascript">
        //<![CDATA[

        window.allow_firefox_cadesplugin_async = 1;

        function isChromiumBased() {
            var retVal = (navigator.userAgent.match(/chrome/i));
            console.log(retVal)
            return retVal;
        }


        function ifUrlThenGet(possibleUrl) {
            if ($.type(possibleUrl) === "string")
                if (possibleUrl.indexOf('http') == 0)
                    $.get(possibleUrl, function (data) {
                        possibleUrl = data;
                    });
            return possibleUrl;
        }

        function signHash(hash, callback) {
            window.xml = false;
            window.dataToSign = ifUrlThenGet(hash);
            window.signCallback = callback;
            PF('signDialog').show();
        }

        function signXml(xml, callback) {
            window.xml = true;
            window.dataToSign = ifUrlThenGet(xml);
            window.signCallback = callback;
            PF('signDialog').show();
        }

        function verifyHashSignature(hash, signature, callback) {
            if (isChromiumBased()) {
                alert('Не реализовано');
            } else {
                VerifyHash(signature, ifUrlThenGet(hash), callback);
            }
        }

        function doSign() {
            if (isChromiumBased() || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Firefox/i) && window.allow_firefox_cadesplugin_async)) {
                if (window.xml)
                    SignCadesXML_Async('certlist', window.dataToSign, window.signCallback);
                else
                    SignCadesBES_Async('certlist', window.dataToSign, window.signCallback);
            } else {
                if (window.xml)
                    SignCadesXML_NPAPI('certlist', window.dataToSign, window.signCallback);
                else
                    SignCadesBES_NPAPI('certlist', window.dataToSign, window.signCallback);
            }
        }

        function onSignShow() {
            $('#signDataTxt').html(window.dataToSign);
            if (isChromiumBased() || (navigator.userAgent.match(/Firefox/i) && window.allow_firefox_cadesplugin_async)) {
                if (navigator.userAgent.match(/Firefox/i) && window.allow_firefox_cadesplugin_async) {
                    nmcades_api_onload();
                }
                CheckForPlugIn_Async('certlist');
            } else {
                CheckForPlugIn_NPAPI('certlist');
            }
        }
